(prog (var n 5)
      (var a (array dim n))
      (print (sizeOf a))
      (print a)
      (var i 0)
      (while (< i (sizeOf a))
             (begin (set (index a i) (- i))
                    (print (index a i))
                    (set i (+ i 1))))
      a)

Program
{
   var n = 5;
   var a = Array[n];
   print( sizeOf(a) );
   print( a );
   var i = 0;
   while (i < sizeOf(a))
   {
      a[i] = -i;
      print( a[i] );
      i = i + 1;
   }
   a;
}

(prog (fun g
           (lambda x (+ 10 x)))
      (fun printArray
           (lambda a
                   (for (var i 0)
                        (< i (sizeOf a))
                        (++ i)
                        (print (index a i)))))
      (fun arrayMap
           (lambda f
                   a
                   (begin (for (var i 0)
                               (< i (sizeOf a))
                               (+++ i)
                               (set (index a i)
                                    (apply f (index a i))))
                          a)))
      (var a (array 2 3 4 5))
      (print a)
      (apply arrayMap g a)
      (print a)
      (apply printArray (apply arrayMap g a))
      a)

Program
{
   g(x)
   {
      10 + x;
   };
   printArray(a)
   {
      for (var i = 0; i < sizeOf(a); i++)
         print( a[i] );;
   };
   arrayMap(f, a)
   {
      for (var i = 0; i < sizeOf(a); ++i)
         a[i] = f(a[i]);;
      a;
   };
   var a = {2, 3, 4, 5};
   print( a );
   arrayMap(g, a);
   print( a );
   printArray(arrayMap(g, a));
   a;
}

3 =========================================
(prog (fun fill
           (lambda a
                   (begin (var i 0)
                          (while (< i (sizeOf a))
                                 (begin (set (index a i) (rand 0 100))
                                        (set i (+ i 1))))
                          a)))
      (fun max
           (lambda a
                   (begin (var m (index a 0))
                          (var i 1)
                          (while (< i (sizeOf a))
                                 (begin (if (< m (index a i))
                                            (set m (index a i))
                                            0)
                                        (set i (+ i 1))))
                          m)))
      (var SIZE 20)
      (apply max
             (print (apply fill (array dim SIZE)))))

Program
{
   fill(a)
   {
      var i = 0;
      while (i < sizeOf(a))
      {
         a[i] = rand(0, 100);
         i = i + 1;
      };
      a;
   };
   max(a)
   {
      var m = a[0];

4 =========================================
(prog (fun fill
           (lambda a
                   (for (var i 0)
                        (< i (sizeOf a))
                        (++ i)
                        (set (index a i) (rand 0 100)))))
      (fun extreme
           (lambda a
                   comp
                   (begin (var m (index a 0))
                          (for (var i 1)
                               (< i (sizeOf a))
                               (++ i)
                               (if (apply comp (index a i) m)
                                   (set m (index a i))
                                   0))
                          m)))
      (fun comp1
           (lambda a b (< a b)))
      (fun comp2
           (lambda a b (> a b)))
      (var SIZE 20)
      (var a (array dim SIZE))
      (apply fill a)
      (print (apply extreme a comp1))
      (print (apply extreme a comp2))
      a)

Program
{
   fill(a)
   {
      for (var i = 0; i < sizeOf(a); i++)
         a[i] = rand(0, 100);;
   };
   extreme(a, comp)
   {
      var m = a[0];
      for (var i = 1; i < sizeOf(a); i++)
         if (comp(a[i], m))
            m = a[i];
         else
            0;;
      m;
   };
   comp1(a, b)
   {
      a < b;
   };
   comp2(a, b)
   {
      a > b;
   };
   var SIZE = 20;
   var a = Array[SIZE];
   fill(a);
   print( extreme(a, comp1) );
   print( extreme(a, comp2) );
   a;
}

(prog (fun fill
           (lambda a
                   (begin (for (var i 0)
                               (< i (sizeOf a))
                               (++ i)
                               (set (index a i) (rand 0 100)))
                          a)))
      (fun sort
           (lambda a
                   comp
                   (begin (var done false)
                          (while (! done)
                                 (begin (set done true)
                                        (for (var i 0)
                                             (< i
                                                (- (sizeOf a) 1))
                                             (++ i)
                                             (if (apply comp
                                                        (index a (+ i 1))
                                                        (index a i))
                                                 (begin (set done false)
                                                        (var temp (index a i))
                                                        (set (index a i)
                                                             (index a (+ i 1)))
                                                        (set (index a (+ i 1))
                                                             temp))
                                                 0))))
                          a)))
      (fun comp1
           (lambda a b (< a b)))
      (fun comp2
           (lambda a b (> a b)))
      (var SIZE 10)
      (var a (array dim SIZE))
      (print (apply fill a))
      (print (apply sort a comp1))
      (print (apply sort a comp2))
      a)

Program
{
   fill(a)
   {
      for (var i = 0; i < sizeOf(a); i++)
         a[i] = rand(0, 100);;
      a;
   };
   sort(a, comp)
   {
      var done = false;
      while (!done)
      {
         done = true;
         for (var i = 0; i < sizeOf(a) - 1; i++)
            if (comp(a[i + 1], a[i]))
            {
               done = false;
               var temp = a[i];
               a[i] = a[i + 1];
               a[i + 1] = temp;
            }
            else
               0;;
      };
      a;
   };
   comp1(a, b)
   {
      a < b;
   };
   comp2(a, b)
   {
      a > b;
   };
   var SIZE = 10;
   var a = Array[SIZE];
   print( fill(a) );
   print( sort(a, comp1) );
   print( sort(a, comp2) );
   a;
}
